		function calcWidth() {
			
			if (!window.matchMedia('(max-width: 991px)').matches) {
				var navwidth = 0;
				var morewidth = $('.header-nav-menu .more').outerWidth(true);
				$('.header-nav-menu > li:not(.more)').each(function() {
					navwidth += $(this).outerWidth( true );
				});
				var availablespace = $('.nav-container').outerWidth(true) - morewidth - 65;

				if (navwidth > availablespace) {
				var lastItem = $('.header-nav-menu > li:not(.more)').last();
				lastItem.attr('data-width', lastItem.outerWidth(true));
				lastItem.addClass('dropdown-menu-item');
				lastItem.removeClass('header-nav-menu-item');
				lastItem.prependTo($('.header-nav-menu .more ul'));
				calcWidth();
				} else {
				var firstMoreElement = $('.header-nav-menu li.more li').first();
				if (navwidth + firstMoreElement.data('width') < availablespace) {
					firstMoreElement.addClass('header-nav-menu-item');
					firstMoreElement.removeClass('dropdown-menu-item');
					firstMoreElement.insertBefore($('.header-nav-menu .more'));
				}
				}

				if ($('.more li').length > 0) {
				$('.more').css('display','inline-block');
				} else {
				$('.more').css('display','none');
				}
			} else{
				$('.header-nav-menu li.more li').each(function(index, val) {
					$(val).addClass('header-nav-menu-item');
					$(val).removeClass('dropdown-menu-item');
					$(val).insertBefore($('.header-nav-menu .more'));
				});
				$('.more').css('display', 'none');
			}
		}
		$(window).on('resize load',function(){
			calcWidth();
		});

		setTimeout(function() {
			$(".nav-container").css("opacity",1);
			$(".nav-container").css("visibility","visible");

		}, 700);

		$('.overlay-search').on('click', function(){
			$('.search-btn').trigger('click')
		})

					url: $(this).attr('data-url')
					// text: 'text'
				}
				navigator.share(data);
			});

		});

	<script type="text/javascript">

		window.addEventListener("scroll", function(){
			showStorieItemsOneByOne();
		});

		var sliderShown = false;
		function showStorieItemsOneByOne()
		{
			var stories = $('.stories-slider')[0];
			var visible = elementInViewport(stories);

			if( visible && !sliderShown )
			{

				var findActive = false;
				var promiseChain = Promise.resolve();
				$(".stories-circle-animation").css({'animation-play-state': 'running'})

				$(".stories-slider .owl-item").each(function (i, item) {

					(function($i, $item) {

						promiseChain = promiseChain.then(function () {


							if( $($item).hasClass("active") )
								findActive = true;

							$($item).css({
								'transform': 'translateY(0)',
								'visibility' : 'visible'
							});

							return new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {
								window.requestAnimationFrame(function () {
									resolve();
								})
							});

						}).then(function () {
							if( findActive  )
							{
								return new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {
									setTimeout(function () {
										resolve();
									}, 55);
								});
							}

						});

					}(i, item));
				});
				sliderShown = true;
			}
		}

		function elementInViewport(el)
		{
			var top = el.offsetTop;
			var left = el.offsetLeft;
			var width = el.offsetWidth;
			var height = el.offsetHeight;

			while(el.offsetParent) {
				el = el.offsetParent;
				top += el.offsetTop;
				left += el.offsetLeft;
			}
			return (
					(top + (height / 2)) < (window.pageYOffset + window.innerHeight) &&
					left < (window.pageXOffset + window.innerWidth) &&
					(top - (height / 2) ) > window.pageYOffset &&
					(left + width) > window.pageXOffset
			);
		}

		$(document).ready(function() {
			var storiesPositionScroll = 0;

				});

				showStorieItemsOneByOne();

			});

			$owl.owlCarousel({
				autoplay: false,
				// autoplayTimeout : 3000,
				loop:true,
				margin:20,
				nav:false,
				dots:false,
				stagePadding: 20,
				responsive:{
					0:{
						items:3,
						margin:20
					},
					600:{
						items:3,
						margin:20
					},
					1000:{
						items:4
					}
				}
			})

			var sync1 = $(".stories-popup-body-slider");
			var sync2 = $(".stories-popup-slider");
			var sync3 = $(".stories-slider");
			var slidesPerPage = 6;
			var syncedSecondary = true;

			sync1.owlCarousel({
				items:1,
				slideSpeed : 2000,
				nav:false,
				autoplay: false,
				// autoplayTimeout: 10000,
				dots:false,
				loop:false,
				margin:10,
				responsiveRefreshRate : 200
			}).on('changed.owl.carousel', syncPosition);

			// sync1.on('changed.owl.carousel', function(e) {
			// 	// sync1.trigger('stop.owl.autoplay');
			// 	// sync1.trigger('play.owl.autoplay');
			// });

			sync2
					.on('initialized.owl.carousel', function () {
						sync2.find(".owl-item").eq(0).addClass("current");
					})
					.owlCarousel({
						items : slidesPerPage,
						dots:false,
						nav:false,
						smartSpeed: 200,
						slideSpeed : 500,
						slideBy: slidesPerPage,
						stagePadding: 20,
						margin:10,
						responsiveRefreshRate : 100
					}).on('changed.owl.carousel', syncPosition2);

			function syncPosition(el) {
				var count = el.item.count-1;
				var current = Math.round(el.item.index - (el.item.count/2) - .5);

				if(current < 0) {
					current = count;
				}
				if(current > count) {
					current = 0;
				}

				sync2
						.find(".owl-item")
						.removeClass("current")
						.eq(el.item.index)
						.addClass("current");
				var onscreen = sync2.find('.owl-item.active').length - 1;
				var start = sync2.find('.owl-item.active').first().index();
				var end = sync2.find('.owl-item.active').last().index();

				sync2.data('owl.carousel').to(el.item.index, 100, true);
			}

			function syncPosition2(el) {
				if(syncedSecondary) {
					var number = el.item.index;
					sync1.data('owl.carousel').to(number, 100, true);
				}
			}

			sync2.on("click", ".owl-item", function(e){
				e.preventDefault();
				var number = $(this).index();
				sync1.data('owl.carousel').to(number, 300, true);
			});


			$('.owl-next').click(function(){
				$('.owl-carousel').trigger('stop.owl.autoplay');
			});

			$("#close-stories").click(function () {
				$('body').removeClass('stories-not-scrolling')
				window.scrollTo(0,storiesPositionScroll)
				$(".stories-popup").hide();
			});

			$(".stories-slider .item").click(function () {

				var dataNum = $(this).attr('data-num');


				storiesPositionScroll = window.pageYOffset
				$(".stories-popup").show();
				$('body').addClass('stories-not-scrolling')
				sync2
						.find(".owl-item")
						.removeClass("current")
						.eq(dataNum)
						.addClass("current");

				sync2.data('owl.carousel').to(dataNum, 100, true);

				sync1.data('owl.carousel').to(dataNum, 300, true);

			});
		});
	</script>

	</a>
